| <span data-ttu-id="f4836-708">Entrada</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4836-708">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="f4836-709">Valor</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4836-709">Value</span></span> |

## <a name="windows-server-2008-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="f4836-1063">Atributos do Windows Server 2008</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4836-1063">Windows Server 2008 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f4836-1064">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2008:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f4836-1064">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2008:</span></span>
